luminity contains an ultrasound contrast agent called perflutren gas . a contrast agent is a medicine used to treat internal body structures . imaging tests include a clearer scan of the heart , ventricle , and echocardiography . it is used as a diagnostic test to make an image of the chest . ultrasound is used to diagnose coronary artery disease . obstruction of the blood vessels supplying the heart muscle . the image is then compared with non - contrast electrocardiography ( e171 ).

tritanrix hepb is a vaccine that protects against four diseases : diphtheria , tetanus ( lockjaw ), pertussis , whooping cough and hepatitis b . the vaccine prevents these diseases from developing . if you have any of these diseases , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . your doctor will decide if the vaccine is right for you . it works by preventing the skin from becoming inflamed or swollen , severe breathing difficulties and suffocation caused by the bacteria - a toxic substance that can cause nerve damage , heart problems and even death .

tritanrix hepb is given as a total of three injections , followed by subsequent injections and a scheduled injection during the complete vaccination course . the vaccine is given by injection into a thigh muscle within 30 minutes of injection . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given the vaccine . your doctor will tell you how many injections to give . you will be given a dose of 3 mg / ml . each dose is given once a day . after each injection , the vaccine will be administered to you via a vein . it is important that you do not have to inject the vaccine in a single dose .

combivir is used to treat hiv ( human immunodeficiency virus ) infection . combivir contains two active ingredients for hiv infection : lamivudine and zidovudini . they are antiretroviral medicines containing nucleoside analogue reverse transcriptase inhibitors ( nrts ). combivir works by reducing the cd4 cell count in your blood . if you have a high number of these cells , your doctor may decide to stop your treatment with combivir . your doctor will decide how to treat your treatment .

micardis belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . they work by causing the body to increase the number of blood vessels to narrow . this can cause your blood pressure to rise . micards blocks the activity of the hormone , which helps the blood vessels relax . it also reduces the risk of the high blood pressure ( essential hypertension ) and helps to lower the amount of blood pressure in your body . low blood pressure can damage blood vessels in several organs , causing heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness , and symptoms of symptoms of stroke .

what zenapax contains the active substance is daclizumab . it belongs to a group of medicines called immunosuppressants . these medicines work by preventing the growth of your transplanted organ . the drug is a humanised monoclonal antibody ( a murine nso myeloma cell line ) called a glucose synthetase , which is produced by the body ' s own glutamine synthesizer . this is used in combination with other antigens , allowing it to bind to an antigen that binds to specific white blood cells , thus preventing transplant rejection . zen apax is used for the treatment of rejecting transplanted kidneys .

temozolomide accord is an anti - cancer medicine used to treat brain tumours . brain tumour ( glioblastoma multiforme ) is a type of brain tumour that can be treated by radiotherapy ( concomitant phase of treatment ) or monotherapy phases of treatment ( i . e . 3 ). if you have a brain tumour , you may need to treat it with a combination of anaplastic or astrocytoma . the cancer cannot be treated with standard therapy .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . if you experience a severe allergic ( hypersensitive ) reaction , such as hives , wheezing or other breathing difficulty , uncontrolled bleeding , seizures ( convulsions ), fever , chills or severe headache , temozolomide sandoz treatment can cause a reduction in certain kinds of blood cells , increased bruising and bleeding ( anaemia ) or red blood cells ( fever ) and reduced resistance to infections . the reduction in blood cell counts may be a sign of anemia ( aplastic anemia ). if any of the above applies to you , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse .
abraxane contains the active substance paclitaxel , which belongs to a group of medicines called taxanes . it works by reducing the amount of the human protein albumin ( a substance that contains tiny particles ) in the blood . the medicine is used to treat cancer , where the cancer is caused by cancer cells , called albumin . when the medicine dissolves , it is released into the blood and into blood vessels . if you experience any of the following side effects , talk to your doctor , pharmacist , nurse or nurse . such side effects are rare and may affect more than one in 10 people .

atazanavir mylan is an antiviral ( antiretroviral ) medicine . it belongs to a group called protease inhibitors . these medicines are used to treat human immunodeficiency virus ( hiv ) infection . hiv is a protein that causes its multiplication , causing the immune system to stop working properly . the active substance is nasopharyngosaccharide , which inhibits the growth of hiv in the body . this helps reduce the risk of developing illnesses and hiv infection in adults and children who are infected with hiv or who have acquired immune deficit syndrome . other anti - hiv medicines are also available in your country . if you are not sure , ask your doctor or pharmacist .

efient contains the active substance prsugrel . it belongs to a group of medicines called anti - platelet agents . platelets are very small cell particles that form in the blood vessel . when they clump , they form a blood clot ( called thrombus ). platelets cause bleeding . if you have a hardened blood vessel called an artery , you may be at risk of a heart attack ( myocardial infarction ), stroke or death . this is because if there is a high chance of clottings in arteries supplying blood to the heart , which reduces the blood supply . unstable angina ( a severe chest pain ) is caused by the clustering of platelets .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . serious side effects common ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) hypoglycaemia low blood sugar cold sweat cool pale skin headache fast heartbeat feeling sick feeling very hungry changes in vision feeling sleepy feeling weak , nervous , anxious , confused , difficulty concentrating , shaking ( tremor ) if you get any of the following symptoms , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse straight away . tell your doctor or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
keep this medicine out of the sight and reach of children . do not use this medicine after the expiry date which is stated on the pen label and carton after exp . store in a refrigerator ( 2 - 8 ). do not freeze . keep the pen in the original package in order to protect from light . the pen cap does not need to be refilled . this medicine should not be disposed of via wastewater or household waste . ask your pharmacist how to dispose of this medicine . these measures will help protect the environment .
what victoza contains the active substance is liraglutide . each pre - filled pen contains 1 ml of solution for injection . the other ingredients are disodium phosphate dihydrate , propylene glycol , phenol , and water for injections . what viktoza looks like and contents of the pack vctoza is a clear , colourless , non - irritant . it is available in packs of 3 , 30 , 0.6% , 15 , 1 , 2 , 5 , 10 or 1 . 8 mm of solution . not all pack sizes may be marketed .
abilify maintaintena contains the active substance aripiprazole . it belongs to a group of medicines called antipsychotics . schizophrenia is a disease with symptoms such as hearing , mistaken beliefs , incoherent speech and behaviour , emotional flatness , depressed , guilty , anxious , and tense . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you start treatment for schizophrenia , you should contact your doctor or pharmacist as soon as possible .
always take abilify maintaintena exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are allergic to aripiprazole or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given this medicine . if any of these apply to you , you should contact your doctor immediately . you may experience suicidal thoughts or behaviours . tell your doctor straight away if your doctor tells you to stop treatment . do not stop treatment immediately , unless you have thoughts or feelings after you have been given . this includes any possible signs of an acutely agitated state or a severely psychootic state heart problems such as stroke , stroke high blood sugar , characterised by symptoms such as excessive thirst , passing of large amounts of urine , increase in appetite or
always use abilify maintaintena exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . the recommended dose for injections is 400 mg , 200 mg or 160 mg once a day . treatment with aripiprazole is given by mouth for 14 days . after 72 hours of treatment , injections are given to the affected area of the gluteal or deltaid muscle , buttock or shoulder . you may experience a little pain after the injection . your doctor will tell you how to administer the injections . if your doctor tells you to stop the injection as soon as possible , the injection will be given to you by a doctor , nurse , pharmacist or nurse .
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . the following side effects may occur with abilify maintaintena : excessive sleepiness , dizziness , confusion , disorientation , difficulty talking or difficulty walking , muscle stiffness or shaking , fever , weakness , irritability , aggression , anxiety , increase in blood pressure , seizures , unconsciousness or unusual movement of the face or tongue . if you notice any of these symptoms , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . for more information on the safety of this medicine , click here .
keep this medicine out of the sight and reach of children . do not use this medicine after the expiry date which is stated on the carton and the reconstituted suspension after exp . this medicine does not require any special storage conditions . store in a refrigerator ( 2 to 8 ). do not freeze . abilify maintaintena should not be disposed of via wastewater or household waste . ask your pharmacist how to dispose of medicines you no longer use . these measures will help protect the environment .
what abilify maintaintena contains - the active substance is aripiprazole . each ml contains 300 mg , after reconstitution and suspension . the other ingredients are : - powder carmellose sodium , mannitol , sodium dihydrogen phosphate monohydrate and sodium hydroxide solvent water . what bilify maintena looks like and contents of the pack abilifying maintainten a is supplied as a powder and solvent , for prolonged - release suspension , in a white powder . it is available in packs containing white powder for a suspension and a spray . not all pack sizes may be marketed .
